Admin Panel Page - **Page Title**: Admin Panel - **Overview**: A page for administrators to manage applications and pets. - **Elements**:   - **ID: admin-panel-page** - Type: Div - Container for the admin panel page.   - **ID: pending-applications** - Type: Div - List of pending adoption applications.   - **ID: all-pets-list** - Type: Div - List of all pets with edit/delete options.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'PetAdoptionCenter' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. User Data - **File Name**: `users.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|email|phone|address   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City   admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave   jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town   ```  ### 2. Pet Data - **File Name**: `pets.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15   2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20   3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01   ```  ### 3. Adoption Applications Data - **File Name**: `applications.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10   2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05   ```  ### 4. Favorites Data - **File Name**: `favorites.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|pet_id|date_added   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|2024-11-01   john_doe|3|2024-11-05   jane_smith|2|2024-10-25   ```  ### 5. Messages Data - **File Name**: `messages.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true   2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false   ```  ### 6. Adoption History Data - **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1   ```  ### 7. Shelters Data - **File Name**: `shelters.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   shelter_id|name|address|phone|email   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com   2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org   ```  All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# Requirements Document for 'PetAdoptionCenter' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'PetAdoptionCenter' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse available pets for adoption, submit adoption applications, manage favorites, and communicate with shelters. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'PetAdoptionCenter' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' web application will consist of the following ten pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Adoption Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured pets, recent activities, and navigation to other functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-pets** - Type: Div - Display of featured pets available for adoption (limit 5).
  - **ID: browse-pets-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to pet listings page.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to refresh dashboard.

### 2. Pet Listings Page
- **Page Title**: Available Pets
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available pets with filtering and search options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-listings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet listings page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search pets by name.
  - **ID: filter-species** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by species (All, Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying pet cards with photo, name, species, and age.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Pet Details Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific pet.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet details page.
  - **ID: pet-name** - Type: H1 - Display pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species** - Type: Div - Display pet species.
  - **ID: pet-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description about the pet.
  - **ID: adopt-button** - Type: Button - Button to start adoption application process.
  - **ID: back-to-listings** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet listings.

### 4. Add Pet Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Pet
- **Overview**: A page for shelter administrators to add new pets for adoption.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-pet-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add pet page.
  - **ID: pet-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select species (Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-breed-input** - Type: Input - Field to input breed.
  - **ID: pet-age-input** - Type: Input - Field to input age (e.g., "2 years").
  - **ID: pet-gender-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select gender (Male, Female).
  - **ID: pet-size-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select size (Small, Medium, Large).
  - **ID: pet-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input detailed description.
  - **ID: submit-pet-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit new pet listing.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 5. Adoption Application Page
- **Page Title**: Adoption Application
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit adoption applications.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: application-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application page.
  - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant's full name.
  - **ID: applicant-phone** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.
  - **ID: housing-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select housing type (House, Apartment, Condo, Other).
  - **ID: reason** - Type: Textarea - Field to explain why they want to adopt this pet.
  - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.
  - **ID: back-to-pet** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet details.

### 6. My Applications Page
- **Page Title**: My Applications
- **Overview**: A page displaying all adoption applications submitted by the user.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: my-applications-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my applications page.
  - **ID: filter-status** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Approved, Rejected).
  - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with pet name, date, status, and actions.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Favorites Page
- **Page Title**: My Favorites
- **Overview**: A page displaying all pets the user has saved as favorites.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.
  - **ID: favorites-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying favorite pet cards.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Messages Page
- **Page Title**: Messages
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and send messages to shelters.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: messages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the messages page.
  - **ID: conversation-list** - Type: Div - List of message conversations.
  - **ID: message-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to compose new message.
  - **ID: send-message-button** - Type: Button - Button to send message.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 9. User Profile Page
- **Page Title**: My Profile
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and edit their profile information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the profile page.
  - **ID: profile-username** - Type: Div - Display username (not editable).
  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Field to update email.
  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to save profile changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 10. Admin Panel Page
- **Page Title**: Admin Panel
- **Overview**: A page for administrators to manage applications and pets.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: admin-panel-page** - Type: Div - Container for the admin panel page.
  - **ID: pending-applications** - Type: Div - List of pending adoption applications.
  - **ID: all-pets-list** - Type: Div - List of all pets with edit/delete options.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email|phone|address
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City
  admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave
  jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town
  ```

### 2. Pet Data
- **File Name**: `pets.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15
  2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20
  3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01
  ```

### 3. Adoption Applications Data
- **File Name**: `applications.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10
  2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05
  ```

### 4. Favorites Data
- **File Name**: `favorites.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|pet_id|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01
  john_doe|3|2024-11-05
  jane_smith|2|2024-10-25
  ```

### 5. Messages Data
- **File Name**: `messages.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true
  2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false
  ```

### 6. Adoption History Data
- **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1
  ```

### 7. Shelters Data
- **File Name**: `shelters.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  shelter_id|name|address|phone|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com
  2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.


  [Agent Output] === design_spec.md ===
# Pet Adoption Web Application Design Specification

## Overview
This document specifies the backend Flask routes and frontend HTML templates for the Pet Adoption web application.

---

## Backend Flask Routes

### Route 1: Dashboard
- **URL:** `/dashboard`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Purpose:** Shows administrative dashboard with summaries of pets, applications, favorites, and messages.

### Route 2: Pet Listings
- **URL:** `/pets`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Purpose:** 
   - GET: Display a list of available pets to browse.
   - POST: Handle filter/search input for pet listings.
- **POST form inputs:**
  - `search_input` (string): Text search for pet name, breed, or type.

### Route 3: Pet Details
- **URL:** `/pets/<int:pet_id>`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Purpose:** Displays detailed information about a specific pet including adoption button.

### Route 4: Applications Page
- **URL:** `/applications`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Purpose:** Lists applications submitted by users, filterable by status.

### Route 5: Favorites Page
- **URL:** `/favorites`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Purpose:** Display a user's list of favorite pets.

### Route 6: Messages Page
- **URL:** `/messages`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Purpose:** Shows messaging conversation list.

---

## Frontend HTML Templates

### Template: dashboard.html
- Summarizes key info such as:
  - Total pets
  - Pending/Approved/Rejected applications
  - Featured pets
  - Recent messages
- **Key Elements and IDs:**
  - Title: `<title>PetAdoptionCenter Dashboard</title>`
  - Dashboard container div: **ID:** `dashboard`
  - Navigation button back to dashboard: **ID:** `back-to-dashboard`

### Template: pets.html
- Displays all pet listings in a grid layout.
- **Key Elements and IDs:**
  - Search input field: **ID:** `search-input`
  - Filter dropdowns (species, age, gender, size): **IDs:** `filter-species`, `pet-age-input`, `pet-gender-input`, `pet-size-input`
  - Pet grid container div: **ID:** `pet-grid`
  - Individual pet cards with data:
    - Name
    - Species
    - Breed
    - Age
    - Gender
    - Size
    - Description
  - Adoption button per pet: **ID:** `adopt-button`
  - Navigation button back to dashboard: **ID:** `back-to-dashboard`

### Template: pet_details.html
- Shows detailed info about a single pet.
- **Key Elements and IDs:**
  - Title: pet name in `<title>` and `<h1>`
  - Description div: **ID:** `pet-description`
  - Age, gender, size, breed, and other info displayed
  - Adoption application button: **ID:** `submit-application-button`
  - Back button: **ID:** `back-to-listings`

### Template: applications.html
- Lists adoption applications.
- **Key Elements and IDs:**
  - Applications table or list: **ID:** `applications-table`
  - Filter status buttons: **ID:** `filter-status`
  - Buttons or links to view application details
  - Back to dashboard button: **ID:** `back-to-dashboard`

### Template: favorites.html
- Displays user's favorite pets in a grid.
- **Key Elements and IDs:**
  - Favorites grid container: **ID:** `favorites-grid`
  - Pet cards similar to pets.html
  - Remove from favorites button: **ID:** `remove-favorite-button`
  - Back to dashboard button: **ID:** `back-to-dashboard`

### Template: messages.html
- Shows conversation list.
- **Key Elements and IDs:**
  - Conversation list div: **ID:** `conversation-list`
  - Button to compose a new message: **ID:** `compose-message-button`
  - Back to dashboard button: **ID:** `back-to-dashboard`

- Pet data fields (from `pets.txt`):
  - `pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added`

- Application data fields (`applications.txt`):

## Notes
- All IDs use lowercase with dashes.
- Use Jinja2 templating for rendering dynamic data.
- Ensure routes use appropriate HTTP methods and redirect after POST.
- All navigation buttons link using `url_for()` Flask method.

This specification enables frontend-backend parallel development with clear interface contracts.

# Requirements Document for 'PetAdoptionCenter' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'PetAdoptionCenter' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse available pets for adoption, submit adoption applications, manage favorites, and communicate with shelters. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'PetAdoptionCenter' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' web application will consist of the following ten pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Adoption Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured pets, recent activities, and navigation to other functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-pets** - Type: Div - Display of featured pets available for adoption (limit 5).
  - **ID: browse-pets-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to pet listings page.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to refresh dashboard.

### 2. Pet Listings Page
- **Page Title**: Available Pets
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available pets with filtering and search options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-listings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet listings page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search pets by name.
  - **ID: filter-species** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by species (All, Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying pet cards with photo, name, species, and age.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Pet Details Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific pet.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet details page.
  - **ID: pet-name** - Type: H1 - Display pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species** - Type: Div - Display pet species.
  - **ID: pet-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description about the pet.
  - **ID: adopt-button** - Type: Button - Button to start adoption application process.
  - **ID: back-to-listings** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet listings.

### 4. Add Pet Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Pet
- **Overview**: A page for shelter administrators to add new pets for adoption.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-pet-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add pet page.
  - **ID: pet-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select species (Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-breed-input** - Type: Input - Field to input breed.
  - **ID: pet-age-input** - Type: Input - Field to input age (e.g., "2 years").
  - **ID: pet-gender-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select gender (Male, Female).
  - **ID: pet-size-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select size (Small, Medium, Large).
  - **ID: pet-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input detailed description.
  - **ID: submit-pet-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit new pet listing.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 5. Adoption Application Page
- **Page Title**: Adoption Application
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit adoption applications.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: application-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application page.
  - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant's full name.
  - **ID: applicant-phone** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.
  - **ID: housing-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select housing type (House, Apartment, Condo, Other).
  - **ID: reason** - Type: Textarea - Field to explain why they want to adopt this pet.
  - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.
  - **ID: back-to-pet** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet details.

### 6. My Applications Page
- **Page Title**: My Applications
- **Overview**: A page displaying all adoption applications submitted by the user.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: my-applications-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my applications page.
  - **ID: filter-status** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Approved, Rejected).
  - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with pet name, date, status, and actions.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Favorites Page
- **Page Title**: My Favorites
- **Overview**: A page displaying all pets the user has saved as favorites.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.
  - **ID: favorites-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying favorite pet cards.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Messages Page
- **Page Title**: Messages
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and send messages to shelters.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: messages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the messages page.
  - **ID: conversation-list** - Type: Div - List of message conversations.
  - **ID: message-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to compose new message.
  - **ID: send-message-button** - Type: Button - Button to send message.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 9. User Profile Page
- **Page Title**: My Profile
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and edit their profile information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the profile page.
  - **ID: profile-username** - Type: Div - Display username (not editable).
  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Field to update email.
  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to save profile changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 10. Admin Panel Page
- **Page Title**: Admin Panel
- **Overview**: A page for administrators to manage applications and pets.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: admin-panel-page** - Type: Div - Container for the admin panel page.
  - **ID: pending-applications** - Type: Div - List of pending adoption applications.
  - **ID: all-pets-list** - Type: Div - List of all pets with edit/delete options.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email|phone|address
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City
  admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave
  jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town
  ```

### 2. Pet Data
- **File Name**: `pets.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15
  2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20
  3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01
  ```

### 3. Adoption Applications Data
- **File Name**: `applications.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10
  2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05
  ```

### 4. Favorites Data
- **File Name**: `favorites.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|pet_id|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01
  john_doe|3|2024-11-05
  jane_smith|2|2024-10-25
  ```

### 5. Messages Data
- **File Name**: `messages.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true
  2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false
  ```

### 6. Adoption History Data
- **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1
  ```

### 7. Shelters Data
- **File Name**: `shelters.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  shelter_id|name|address|phone|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com
  2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# Pet Adoption Web Application Design Specification

## Overview
This document specifies the backend Flask routes and frontend HTML templates for the Pet Adoption web application.

---

## Backend Flask Routes

### Route 1: Dashboard
- **URL:** `/dashboard`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Purpose:** Shows administrative dashboard with summaries of pets, applications, favorites, and messages.

### Route 2: Pet Listings
- **URL:** `/pets`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Purpose:** 
   - GET: Display a list of available pets to browse.
   - POST: Handle filter/search input for pet listings.
- **POST form inputs:**
  - `search_input` (string): Text search for pet name, breed, or type.

### Route 3: Pet Details
- **URL:** `/pets/<int:pet_id>`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Purpose:** Displays detailed information about a specific pet including adoption button.

### Route 4: Applications Page
- **URL:** `/applications`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Purpose:** Lists applications submitted by users, filterable by status.

### Route 5: Favorites Page
- **URL:** `/favorites`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Purpose:** Display a user's list of favorite pets.

### Route 6: Messages Page
- **URL:** `/messages`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Purpose:** Shows messaging conversation list.

---

## Frontend HTML Templates

### Template: dashboard.html
- Summarizes key info such as:
  - Total pets
  - Pending/Approved/Rejected applications

`size` (str): Size category (Small, Medium, Large)\n  - `description` (str): Text description\n  - `shelter_id` (int): Shelter identifier\n  - `status` (str): Availability status (Available, Pending, Adopted)\n  - # Requirements Document for 'PetAdoptionCenter' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'PetAdoptionCenter' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse available pets for adoption, submit adoption applications, manage favorites, and communicate with shelters. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'PetAdoptionCenter' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' web application will consist of the following ten pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Adoption Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured pets, recent activities, and navigation to other functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-pets** - Type: Div - Display of featured pets available for adoption (limit 5).
  - **ID: browse-pets-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to pet listings page.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to refresh dashboard.

### 2. Pet Listings Page
- **Page Title**: Available Pets
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available pets with filtering and search options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-listings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet listings page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search pets by name.
  - **ID: filter-species** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by species (All, Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying pet cards with photo, name, species, and age.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Pet Details Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific pet.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet details page.
  - **ID: pet-name** - Type: H1 - Display pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species** - Type: Div - Display pet species.
  - **ID: pet-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description about the pet.
  - **ID: adopt-button** - Type: Button - Button to start adoption application process.
  - **ID: back-to-listings** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet listings.

### 4. Add Pet Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Pet
- **Overview**: A page for shelter administrators to add new pets for adoption.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-pet-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add pet page.
  - **ID: pet-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select species (Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-breed-input** - Type: Input - Field to input breed.
  - **ID: pet-age-input** - Type: Input - Field to input age (e.g., "2 years").
  - **ID: pet-gender-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select gender (Male, Female).
  - **ID: pet-size-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select size (Small, Medium, Large).
  - **ID: pet-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input detailed description.
  - **ID: submit-pet-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit new pet listing.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 5. Adoption Application Page
- **Page Title**: Adoption Application
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit adoption applications.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: application-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application page.
  - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant's full name.
  - **ID: applicant-phone** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.
  - **ID: housing-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select housing type (House, Apartment, Condo, Other).
  - **ID: reason** - Type: Textarea - Field to explain why they want to adopt this pet.
  - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.
  - **ID: back-to-pet** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet details.

### 6. My Applications Page
- **Page Title**: My Applications
- **Overview**: A page displaying all adoption applications submitted by the user.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: my-applications-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my applications page.
  - **ID: filter-status** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Approved, Rejected).
  - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with pet name, date, status, and actions.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Favorites Page
- **Page Title**: My Favorites
- **Overview**: A page displaying all pets the user has saved as favorites.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.
  - **ID: favorites-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying favorite pet cards.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Messages Page
- **Page Title**: Messages
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and send messages to shelters.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: messages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the messages page.
  - **ID: conversation-list** - Type: Div - List of message conversations.
  - **ID: message-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to compose new message.
  - **ID: send-message-button** - Type: Button - Button to send message.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 9. User Profile Page
- **Page Title**: My Profile
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and edit their profile information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the profile page.
  - **ID: profile-username** - Type: Div - Display username (not editable).
  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Field to update email.
  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to save profile changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 10. Admin Panel Page
- **Page Title**: Admin Panel
- **Overview**: A page for administrators to manage applications and pets.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: admin-panel-page** - Type: Div - Container for the admin panel page.
  - **ID: pending-applications** - Type: Div - List of pending adoption applications.
  - **ID: all-pets-list** - Type: Div - List of all pets with edit/delete options.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email|phone|address
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City
  admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave
  jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town
  ```

### 2. Pet Data
- **File Name**: `pets.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15
  2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20
  3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01
  ```

### 3. Adoption Applications Data
- **File Name**: `applications.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10
  2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05
  ```

### 4. Favorites Data
- **File Name**: `favorites.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|pet_id|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01
  john_doe|3|2024-11-05
  jane_smith|2|2024-10-25
  ```

### 5. Messages Data
- **File Name**: `messages.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true
  2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false
  ```

### 6. Adoption History Data
- **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1
  ```

### 7. Shelters Data
- **File Name**: `shelters.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  shelter_id|name|address|phone|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com
  2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# Pet Adoption Web Application Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Backend Flask Routes

### 1. Root Redirect
- **URL:** `/`
- **Function:** `root_redirect`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Behavior:** Redirects to `/dashboard`

### 2. Dashboard
- **URL:** `/dashboard`
- **Function:** `dashboard`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Template:** `dashboard.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `total_pets` (int): Number of pets in system
  - `pending_applications` (int): Count of pending adoption applications
  - `approved_applications` (int): Count of approved adoption applications
  - `featured_pets` (list of dict): List of featured pets with keys: `pet_id` (int), `name` (str), `species` (str), `breed` (str), `age` (int), `gender` (str), `size` (str), `description` (str)
  - `recent_messages` (list of dict): List of latest messages with keys: `message_id` (int), `sender_username` (str), `subject` (str), `timestamp` (str)

### 3. Pets Listing
- **URL:** `/pets`
- **Function:** `pets_listing`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Templates:** `pets.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `pets` (list of dict): List of pets; each dict keys:
    - `pet_id` (int), `name` (str), `species` (str), `breed` (str), `age` (int), `gender` (str), `size` (str), `description` (str), `status` (str), `date_added` (str)
  - `filter_species` (str, optional): Current species filter value
  - `filter_age` (str, optional): Current age filter
  - `filter_gender` (str, optional): Current gender filter
  - `filter_size` (str, optional): Current size filter
- **POST Form Fields:**
  - `search_input` (str): Text for searching pet listings
  - `filter_species` (str)
  - `filter_age` (str)
  - `filter_gender` (str)
  - `filter_size` (str)

### 4. Pet Details
- **URL:** `/pets/<int:pet_id>`
- **Function:** `pet_details`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Template:** `pet_details.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `pet` (dict): Pet information with keys:
    - `pet_id` (int), `name` (str), `species` (str), `breed` (str), `age` (int), `gender` (str), `size` (str), `description` (str), `status` (str), `date_added` (str), `shelter_id` (int)

### 5. Applications Listing
- **URL:** `/applications`
- **Function:** `applications_listing`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Template:** `applications.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `applications` (list of dict): Each dict keys:
    - `application_id` (int), `username` (str), `pet_id` (int), `applicant_name` (str), `phone` (str), `address` (str), `housing_type` (str), `has_yard` (bool), `other_pets` (str), `experience` (str), `reason` (str), `status` (str), `date_submitted` (str)
  - `filter_status` (str, optional): Current filter for application status

### 6. Favorites Page
- **URL:** `/favorites`
- **Function:** `favorites_page`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Template:** `favorites.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `favorites` (list of dict): Pet data similar structure to pet listings

### 7. Messages Page
- **URL:** `/messages`
- **Function:** `messages_page`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Template:** `messages.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `conversations` (list of dict): Each dict keys:
    - `message_id` (int), `sender_username` (str), `recipient_username` (str), `subject` (str), `content` (str), `timestamp` (str), `is_read` (bool)

---

## Section 2: Frontend HTML Templates

### 1. dashboard.html
- **File path:** `templates/dashboard.html`
- **Title:** `PetAdoptionCenter Dashboard`
- **H1 header:** `Dashboard`
- **IDs and Elements:**
  - `<div id="dashboard">` container
  - `<button id="back-to-dashboard"` for navigation back
  - Displays statistics using passed context variables (e.g., total pets, featured pets)

### 2. pets.html
- **File path:** `templates/pets.html`
- **Title:** `Browse Pets - PetAdoptionCenter`
- **H1 header:** `Available Pets`
- **IDs and Elements:**
  - `<input id="search-input" type="text" name="search_input">` for search filter
  - Dropdown filters:
    - Species: `<select id="filter-species" name="filter_species">`
    - Age: `<select id="pet-age-input" name="filter_age">`
    - Gender: `<select id="pet-gender-input" name="filter_gender">`
    - Size: `<select id="pet-size-input" name="filter_size">`
  - `<div id="pet-grid">` container displaying pet cards
  - Each pet card includes pet info and:
    - `<button id="adopt-button-{{ pet.pet_id }}">Adopt</button>`
  - Navigation button:
    - `<button id="back-to-dashboard"` using `url_for('dashboard')`

### 3. pet_details.html
- **File path:** `templates/pet_details.html`
- **Title:** `{{ pet.name }} - Pet Details`
- **H1 header:** `{{ pet.name }}`
- **IDs and Elements:**
  - `<div id="pet-description">` showing pet.description
  - Fields for age, gender, size, breed
  - `<button id="submit-application-button">Apply to Adopt</button>`
  - `<button id="back-to-listings">Back to Listings</button>`

### 4. applications.html
- **File path:** `templates/applications.html`
- **Title:** `Adoption Applications`
- **H1 header:** `Applications`
- **IDs and Elements:**
  - `<table id="applications-table">` listing applications
  - Filter buttons:
    - `<button id="filter-status" ...>` to filter by application status
  - Navigation button:
    - `<button id="back-to-dashboard">Dashboard</button>`

### 5. favorites.html
- **File path:** `templates/favorites.html`
- **Title:** `My Favorite Pets`
- **H1 header:** `Favorites`
- **IDs and Elements:**
  - `<div id="favorites-grid">` container
  - Each favorite pet card with remove button:
    - `<button id="remove-favorite-button-{{ pet.pet_id }}">Remove</button>`
  - Navigation button:
    - `<button id="back-to-dashboard">Dashboard</button>`

### 6. messages.html
- **File path:** `templates/messages.html`
- **Title:** `Messages`
- **H1 header:** `Messages`
- **IDs and Elements:**
  - `<div id="conversation-list">` listing conversations
  - `<button id="compose-message-button">Compose</button>`
  - `<button id="back-to-dashboard">Dashboard</button>`

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. pets.txt
- **Fields (pipe-delimited order):**
  `pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added`
- **Descriptions:**
  - `pet_id` (int): Unique pet identifier
  - `name` (str): Pet name
  - `species` (str): Species (e.g., Dog, Cat, Bird)
  - `breed` (str): Breed of the pet
  - `age` (int): Age in years
  - `gender` (str): Gender (Male, Female)
  - `size` (str): Size category (Small, Medium, Large)
  - `description` (str): Text description
  - `shelter_id` (int): Shelter identifier
  - `status` (str): Availability status (Available, Pending, Adopted)
  - `date_added` (str): ISO date string (YYYY-MM-DD)
- **Example row:**
  `1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|5|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic|2|Available|2024-11-01`

### 2. applications.txt
- **Fields:**
  `application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted`
- **Descriptions:**
  - `application_id` (int): Unique application ID
  - `username` (str): Username who applied
  - `pet_id` (int): Pet id applied for
  - `applicant_name` (str): Full name of applicant
  - `phone` (str): Contact phone
  - `address` (str): Applicant address
  - `housing_type` (str): Type of housing (House, Apartment, etc.)
  - `has_yard` (bool): Indicates if yard available
  - `other_pets` (str): Info about other pets
  - `experience` (str): Pet ownership experience
  - `reason` (str): Reason for adoption
  - `status` (str): Application status (Pending, Approved, Rejected)
  - `date_submitted` (str): Date of submission
- **Example row:**
  `7|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak St|Apartment|No|None|First time adopter|Pending|2024-11-10`

### 3. favorites.txt
- **Fields:**
  `username|pet_id|date_added`
- **Example row:**
  `john_doe|1|2024-11-15`

### 4. messages.txt
- **Fields:**
  `message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read`
- **Example row:**
  `1|john_doe|admin_user|Question|When can I visit?|2024-11-05 14:30:00|false`

### 5. users.txt
- **Fields:**
  `username|email|phone|address|role`
- **Example row:**
  `admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Pet St|admin`

### 6. shelters.txt
- **Fields:**
  `shelter_id|name|address|phone|email`
- **Example row:**
  `2|Second Chance Shelter|100 Main Rd|555-2000|info@secondchance.org`

### 7. adoption_history.txt
- **Fields:**
  `history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id`
- **Example row:**
  `1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-10-25|1`

---

## Additional Notes
- All frontend navigation buttons use Flask's `url_for()` to dynamically generate URLs.
- Data files stored in `data/` directory.
- All IDs and variables follow lowercase with dashes or underscores as appropriate for HTML and Python.
- Templates use Jinja2 for variable substitutions.
- POST routes redirect after successful form processing to ensure safe reload.

This comprehensive specification supports parallel independent development of backend Flask routes and frontend HTML templates with consistent data schema definitions.

## 1. Objective

The required development language for the 'PetAdoptionCenter' application is Python.

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' web application will consist of the following ten pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Adoption Dashboard

## 4. Data Storage

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email|phone|address
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City
  admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave
  jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town
  ```

### 2. Pet Data
- **File Name**: `pets.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15
  2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20
  3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01
  ```

### 3. Adoption Applications Data
- **File Name**: `applications.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10
  2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05
  ```

### 4. Favorites Data
- **File Name**: `favorites.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|pet_id|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01
  john_doe|3|2024-11-05
  jane_smith|2|2024-10-25
  ```

### 5. Messages Data
- **File Name**: `messages.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true
  2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false
  ```

### 6. Adoption History Data
- **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1
  ```

### 7. Shelters Data
- **File Name**: `shelters.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  shelter_id|name|address|phone|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com
  2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. pets.txt
- **Fields (pipe-delimited order):**
  `pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added`
- **Descriptions:**
  - `pet_id` (int): Unique pet identifier
  - `name` (str): Pet name
  - `species` (str): Species (e.g., Dog, Cat, Bird)
  - `breed` (str): Breed of the pet
  - `age` (int): Age in years
  - `gender` (str): Gender (Male, Female)
  - `size` (str): Size category (Small, Medium, Large)
  - `description` (str): Text description
  - `shelter_id` (int): Shelter identifier
  - `status` (str): Availability status (Available, Pending, Adopted)
  - `date_added` (str): ISO date string (YYYY-MM-DD)
- **Example row:**
  `1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|5|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic|2|Available|2024-11-01`

### 2. applications.txt
- **Fields:**
  `application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted`
- **Descriptions:**
  - `application_id` (int): Unique application ID
  - `username` (str): Username who applied
  - `pet_id` (int): Pet id applied for
  - `applicant_name` (str): Full name of applicant
  - `phone` (str): Contact phone
  - `address` (str): Applicant address
  - `housing_type` (str): Type of housing (House, Apartment, etc.)
  - `has_yard` (bool): Indicates if yard available
  - `other_pets` (str): Info about other pets
  - `experience` (str): Pet ownership experience
  - `reason` (str): Reason for adoption
  - `status` (str): Application status (Pending, Approved, Rejected)
  - `date_submitted` (str): Date of submission
- **Example row:**
  `7|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak St|Apartment|No|None|First time adopter|Pending|2024-11-10`

### 3. favorites.txt
- **Fields:**
  `username|pet_id|date_added`
- **Example row:**
  `john_doe|1|2024-11-15`

### 4. messages.txt
- **Fields:**
  `message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read`
- **Example row:**
  `1|john_doe|admin_user|Question|When can I visit?|2024-11-05 14:30:00|false`

### 5. users.txt
- **Fields:**
  `username|email|phone|address|role`
- **Example row:**
  `admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Pet St|admin`

### 6. shelters.txt
- **Fields:**
  `shelter_id|name|address|phone|email`
- **Example row:**
  `2|Second Chance Shelter|100 Main Rd|555-2000|info@secondchance.org`

### 7. adoption_history.txt
- **Fields:**
  `history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id`
- **Example row:**
  `1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-10-25|1`

# Requirements Document for 'PetAdoptionCenter' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'PetAdoptionCenter' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse available pets for adoption, submit adoption applications, manage favorites, and communicate with shelters. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'PetAdoptionCenter' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' web application will consist of the following ten pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Adoption Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured pets, recent activities, and navigation to other functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-pets** - Type: Div - Display of featured pets available for adoption (limit 5).
  - **ID: browse-pets-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to pet listings page.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to refresh dashboard.

### 2. Pet Listings Page
- **Page Title**: Available Pets
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available pets with filtering and search options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-listings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet listings page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search pets by name.
  - **ID: filter-species** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by species (All, Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying pet cards with photo, name, species, and age.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Pet Details Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific pet.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet details page.
  - **ID: pet-name** - Type: H1 - Display pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species** - Type: Div - Display pet species.
  - **ID: pet-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description about the pet.
  - **ID: adopt-button** - Type: Button - Button to start adoption application process.
  - **ID: back-to-listings** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet listings.

### 4. Add Pet Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Pet
- **Overview**: A page for shelter administrators to add new pets for adoption.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-pet-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add pet page.
  - **ID: pet-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select species (Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-breed-input** - Type: Input - Field to input breed.
  - **ID: pet-age-input** - Type: Input - Field to input age (e.g., "2 years").
  - **ID: pet-gender-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select gender (Male, Female).
  - **ID: pet-size-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select size (Small, Medium, Large).
  - **ID: pet-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input detailed description.
  - **ID: submit-pet-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit new pet listing.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 5. Adoption Application Page
- **Page Title**: Adoption Application
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit adoption applications.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: application-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application page.
  - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant's full name.
  - **ID: applicant-phone** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.
  - **ID: housing-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select housing type (House, Apartment, Condo, Other).
  - **ID: reason** - Type: Textarea - Field to explain why they want to adopt this pet.
  - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.
  - **ID: back-to-pet** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet details.

### 6. My Applications Page
- **Page Title**: My Applications
- **Overview**: A page displaying all adoption applications submitted by the user.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: my-applications-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my applications page.
  - **ID: filter-status** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Approved, Rejected).
  - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with pet name, date, status, and actions.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Favorites Page
- **Page Title**: My Favorites
- **Overview**: A page displaying all pets the user has saved as favorites.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.
  - **ID: favorites-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying favorite pet cards.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Messages Page
- **Page Title**: Messages
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and send messages to shelters.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: messages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the messages page.
  - **ID: conversation-list** - Type: Div - List of message conversations.
  - **ID: message-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to compose new message.
  - **ID: send-message-button** - Type: Button - Button to send message.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 9. User Profile Page
- **Page Title**: My Profile
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and edit their profile information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the profile page.
  - **ID: profile-username** - Type: Div - Display username (not editable).
  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Field to update email.
  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to save profile changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 10. Admin Panel Page
- **Page Title**: Admin Panel
- **Overview**: A page for administrators to manage applications and pets.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: admin-panel-page** - Type: Div - Container for the admin panel page.
  - **ID: pending-applications** - Type: Div - List of pending adoption applications.
  - **ID: all-pets-list** - Type: Div - List of all pets with edit/delete options.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email|phone|address
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City
  admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave
  jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town
  ```

### 2. Pet Data
- **File Name**: `pets.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15
  2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20
  3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01
  ```

### 3. Adoption Applications Data
- **File Name**: `applications.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10
  2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05
  ```

### 4. Favorites Data
- **File Name**: `favorites.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|pet_id|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01
  john_doe|3|2024-11-05
  jane_smith|2|2024-10-25
  ```

### 5. Messages Data
- **File Name**: `messages.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true
  2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false
  ```

### 6. Adoption History Data
- **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1
  ```

### 7. Shelters Data
- **File Name**: `shelters.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  shelter_id|name|address|phone|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com
  2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

`pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added`\n\n- Application data fields (`applications.txt`):\n  - `application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted`\n\n- Users: username, email, phone, address, role (admin/user)\n\n- Shelters: shelter_id|name|address|phone|email\n\n\n---\n\n## Notes\n- All IDs use lowercase with dashes.\n- Use Jinja2 templating for rendering dynamic data.\n- Ensure routes use appropriate HTTP methods and redirect after POST.\n- All navigation buttons link using `url_for()` Flask method.\n\nThis specification enables frontend-backend parallel development with clear interface contracts."})

  history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id

  1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1

- **Data Format**:
  ```
  shelter_id|name|address|phone|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com
  2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

Data Storage  The 'PetAdoptionCenter' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. User Data - **File Name**: `users.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|email|phone|address   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City   admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave   jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town   ```  ### 2. Pet Data - **File Name**: `pets.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15   2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20   3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01   ```  ### 3. Favorites Data - **File Name**: `favorites.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|pet_id|date_added   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|2024-11-01   john_doe|3|2024-11-05   jane_smith|2|2024-10-25   ```  ### 5. Messages Data - **File Name**: `messages.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true   2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false   ```  ### 6. Adoption History Data - **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1   ```  ### 7. Shelters Data - **File Name**: `shelters.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   shelter_id|name|address|phone|email   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com   2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org   ```  All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

`all_pets` (List[Dict])\n\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas (Backend Focus)\n\n### 1. users.txt\n- **File Path:** `data/users.txt`\n- **Fields (pipe-delimited):**\n  `username|email|phone|address`\n- **Field Descriptions:**\n  - `username` (str): Unique user identifier.\n  - `email` (str): User email address.\n  - `phone` (str): Phone number.\n  - `address` (str): User full address.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City\n  admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave\n  jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town\n  ```\n\n### 2. pets.txt\n- **File Path:** `data/pets.txt`\n- **Fields:**\n  `pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added`\n- **Field Descriptions:**\n  - `pet_id` (int): Unique pet ID.\n  - `name` (str): Pet's name.\n  - `species` (str): Species (Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).\n  - `breed` (str): Breed name.\n  - `age` (str): Age in years with units (e.g., \"3 years\").\n  - `gender` (str): Male or Female.\n  - `size` (str): Small, Medium, Large.\n  - `description` (str): Detailed pet description.\n  - `shelter_id` (int): Shelter unique ID.\n  - `status` (str): Pet availability status (Available, Pending, Adopted).\n  - `date_added` (str): Date in ISO format (YYYY-MM-DD).\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15\n  2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20\n  3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01\n  ```\n\n### 3. applications.txt\n- **File Path:** `data/applications.txt`\n- **Fields:**\n  `application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted`\n- **Field Descriptions:**\n  - `application_id` (int): Unique application ID.\n  - `username` (str): User submitting application.\n  - `pet_id` (int): Pet applied for.\n  - `applicant_name` (str): Full name.\n  - `phone` (str): Contact phone.\n  - `address` (str): Full address.\n  - `housing_type` (str): House, Apartment, Condo, Other.\n  - `has_yard` (bool): Yes or No.\n  - `other_pets` (str): Description.\n  - `experience` (str): Years or description.\n  - `reason` (str): Reason to adopt.\n  - `status` (str): Pending, Approved, Rejected.\n  - `date_submitted` (str): ISO date.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10\n  2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05\n  ```\n\n### 4. favorites.txt\n- **File Path:** `data/favorites.txt`\n- **Fields:**\n  `username|pet_id|date_added`\n- **Field Descriptions:**\n  - `username` (str): User's username.\n  - `pet_id` (int): Pet favorited.\n  - `date_added` (str): Date added to favorites.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  john_doe|1|2024-11-01\n  john_doe|3|2024-11-05\n  jane_smith|2|2024-10-25\n  ```\n\n### 5. messages.txt\n- **File Path:** `data/messages.txt`\n- **Fields:**\n  `message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read`\n- **Field Descriptions:**\n  - `message_id` (int): Unique message ID.\n  - `sender_username` (str): Username of sender.\n  - `recipient_username` (str): Username of recipient.\n  - `subject` (str): Message subject.\n  - `content` (str): Full message content.\n  - `timestamp` (str): DateTime ISO format.\n  - `is_read` (bool): True or False.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true\n  2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false\n  ```\n\n### 6. adoption_history.txt\n- **File Path:** `data/adoption_history.txt`\n- **Fields:**\n  `history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id`\n- **Field Descriptions:**\n  - `history_id` (int): Unique id\n  - `username` (str): User who adopted\n  - `pet_id` (int): Pet id adopted\n  - `pet_name` (str): Pet name\n  - `adoption_date` (str): ISO date\n  - `shelter_id` (int): Shelter id\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1\n  ```\n\n### 7. shelters.txt\n- **File Path:** `data/shelters.txt`\n- **Fields:**\n  `shelter_id|name|address|phone|email`\n- **Field Descriptions:**\n  - `shelter_id` (int): Unique shelter id\n  - `name` (str): Shelter name\n  - `address` (str): Shelter location\n  - `phone` (str): Contact phone\n  - `email` (str): Contact email\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com\n  2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org\n  ```\n\n---\n\n# End of Design Specification\n\nThis specification enables independent backend and frontend development aligned exclusively by these clear, detailed interfaces."})

`pet_id` (int): Unique pet ID\n  - `name` (str): Pet name\n  - `species` (str): Species (Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other)\n  - `breed` (str): Breed\n  - `age` (str): Age with unit (e.g., \"3 years\")\n  - `gender` (str): Male or Female\n  - `size` (str): Small, Medium, or Large\n  - `description` (str): Detailed description\n  - `shelter_id` (int): Shelter identifier\n  - `status` (str): Availability status (Available, Pending, Adopted)\n  - `date_added` (str): Date added (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15\n  2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20\n  3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01\n  ```\n\n### 3. applications.txt\n- **File Path:** `data/applications.txt`\n- **Fields:**\n  `application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted`\n- **Field Descriptions:**\n  - `application_id` (int): Unique application ID\n  - `username` (str): Applicant's username\n  - `pet_id` (int): Target pet ID\n  - `applicant_name` (str): Applicant's full name\n  - `phone` (str): Contact phone\n  - `address` (str): Applicant's address\n  - `housing_type` (str): Housing type\n  - `has_yard` (str): \"Yes\" or \"No\"\n  - `other_pets` (str): Description of other pets\n  - `experience` (str): Pet experience\n  - `reason` (str): Reason for applying\n  - `status` (str): Application status (Pending, Approved, Rejected)\n  - `date_submitted` (str): Date submitted (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10\n  2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05\n  ```\n\n### 4. favorites.txt\n- **File Path:** `data/favorites.txt`\n- **Fields:**\n  `username|pet_id|date_added`\n- **Field Descriptions:**\n  - `username` (str): User's username\n  - `pet_id` (int): Pet favorited\n  - `date_added` (str): Date when favorited\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  john_doe|1|2024-11-01\n  john_doe|3|2024-11-05\n  jane_smith|2|2024-10-25\n  ```\n\n### 5. messages.txt\n- **File Path:** `data/messages.txt`\n- **Fields:**\n  `message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read`\n- **Field Descriptions:**\n  - `message_id` (int): Unique message ID\n  - `sender_username` (str): Sender username\n  - `recipient_username` (str): Recipient username\n  - `subject` (str): Message subject\n  - `content` (str): Message body\n  - `timestamp` (str): Date and time (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS)\n  - `is_read` (bool): true/false\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true\n  2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false\n  ```\n\n### 6. adoption_history.txt\n- **File Path:** `data/adoption_history.txt`\n- **Fields:**\n  `history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id`\n- **Field Descriptions:**\n  - `history_id` (int): Unique ID\n  - `username` (str): Adopter username\n  - `pet_id` (int): Pet ID\n  - `pet_name` (str): Pet name\n  - `adoption_date` (str): Date adopted\n  - `shelter_id` (int): Shelter ID\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1\n  ```\n\n### 7. shelters.txt\n- **File Path:** `data/shelters.txt`\n- **Fields:**\n  `shelter_id|name|address|phone|email`\n- **Field Descriptions:**\n  - `shelter_id` (int): Unique shelter ID\n  - `name` (str): Shelter name\n  - `address` (str): Shelter address\n  - `phone` (str): Contact phone\n  - `email` (str): Contact email\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com\n  2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org\n  ```\n\n---\n\nEnd of Design Specification.\n\nThis document defines comprehensive backend routes, frontend templates, and data schemas to allow fully independent development of the PetAdoptionCenter application.\n"})
